<a id="15020" class="Comment">-- An element of the poset is like a finite observation whereas an element of the</a>
<a id="15102" class="Comment">-- frame of downward closed posets is like a general observation.</a>

<a id="15169" class="Comment">-- The set of downward-closed subsets of a poset forms a frame.</a>

<a id="24479" class="Comment">-- Similar to the poset case, this is sufficient to establish that the category of frames</a>
<a id="24569" class="Comment">-- is univalent</a>

<a id="‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°"></a><a id="24586" href="Frame.html#24586" class="Function">‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°</a> <a id="24591" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24593" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24594" href="Frame.html#24594" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="24596" href="Frame.html#24596" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="24598" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24600" href="Frame.html#3257" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="24606" href="Basis.html#2320" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="24609" href="Basis.html#2323" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="24612" href="Basis.html#2326" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÇ</a><a id="24614" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24616" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="24618" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24619" href="Frame.html#24594" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="24621" href="Frame.html#22064" class="Function Operator">‚âÉf</a> <a id="24624" href="Frame.html#24596" class="Bound">G</a><a id="24625" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24627" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Glue.html#1051" class="Function Operator">‚âÉ</a> <a id="24629" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24630" href="Frame.html#24594" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="24632" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="24634" href="Frame.html#24596" class="Bound">G</a><a id="24635" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="24637" href="Frame.html#24586" class="Function">‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°</a> <a id="24642" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24644" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#4416" class="Function">SIP</a> <a id="24648" href="Frame.html#24353" class="Function">frame-is-univ-str</a>

<a id="24667" class="Comment">-- However, there are two minor issues with this.</a>
<a id="24717" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="24720" class="Comment">--   1. We do not have to talk about equivalences as we are talking about sets;</a>
<a id="24800" class="Comment">--      isomorphisms are well-behaved in our case as we are dealing with sets.</a>
<a id="24879" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="24882" class="Comment">--  2. We do not have to require the frame data to be preserved. We can show that any</a>
<a id="24968" class="Comment">--     poset isomorphism preserves the frame operators.</a>
<a id="25024" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="25027" class="Comment">-- We will therefore strengthen our result to work with the notion of poset isomorphism.</a>

<a id="25117" class="Comment">-- We start by showing the equivalence between ‚âÉf and ‚âÖ‚Çö.</a>

<a id="‚âÉf‚âÉ‚âÖ‚Çö"></a><a id="25176" href="Frame.html#25176" class="Function">‚âÉf‚âÉ‚âÖ‚Çö</a> <a id="25182" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25184" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25185" href="Frame.html#25185" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="25187" href="Frame.html#25187" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="25189" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25191" href="Frame.html#3257" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="25197" href="Basis.html#2320" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="25200" href="Basis.html#2323" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="25203" href="Basis.html#2326" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÇ</a><a id="25205" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25207" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="25209" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25210" href="Frame.html#3524" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="25214" href="Frame.html#25185" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="25216" href="Poset.html#15630" class="Function Operator">‚âÖ‚Çö</a> <a id="25219" href="Frame.html#3524" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="25223" href="Frame.html#25187" class="Bound">G</a><a id="25224" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25226" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Glue.html#1051" class="Function Operator">‚âÉ</a> <a id="25228" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25229" href="Frame.html#25185" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="25231" href="Frame.html#22064" class="Function Operator">‚âÉf</a> <a id="25234" href="Frame.html#25187" class="Bound">G</a><a id="25235" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="30618" class="Comment">-- Now that we have this result, we can move on to show that given two frames F and G,</a>
<a id="30705" class="Comment">-- (pos F) ‚âÖ‚Çö (pos G) is equivalent to F ‚â° G.</a>
